CREATE TABLE DNA ( id INT PRIMARY KEY, sequence TEXT NOT NULL, type VARCHAR(50) )

CREATE TABLE GeneExpression ( id INT PRIMARY KEY, gene_id INT NOT NULL, level FLOAT NOT NULL, FOREIGN KEY (gene_id) REFERENCES Gene(id) )</t><s>INSERT INTO Gene (id, name, sequence, location) VALUES (1, 'GeneA', 'ATCG', 'Chr1') ON CONFLICT (id) DO UPDATE SET name=EXCLUDED.name, sequence=EXCLUDED.sequence, location=EXCLUDED.location</s>
